
GNG_worsen_corruption = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = GNG_corruption_asias_finest_dummy
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_status_var_temp = 2 }
		GNG_update_corruption = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = GNG_corruption_corrupt_dummy
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_status_var_temp = 0 }
		GNG_update_corruption = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = GNG_corruption_passable_dummy
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_status_var_temp = 1 }
		GNG_update_corruption = yes
	}
}
GNG_worsen_corruption_2 = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = GNG_corruption_asias_finest_dummy
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_status_var_temp = 1 }
		GNG_update_corruption = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = GNG_corruption_corrupt_dummy
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_status_var_temp = 0 }
		GNG_update_corruption = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = GNG_corruption_passable_dummy
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_status_var_temp = 0 }
		GNG_update_corruption = yes
	}
}

GNG_check_votes_legco = {
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_legco_faction_support^1
		min = 0
		max = GNG_legco_yasuda_seats
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_legco_faction_support^2
		min = 0
		max = GNG_legco_suzuki_seats
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_legco_faction_support^3
		min = 0
		max = GNG_legco_sony_seats
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_legco_faction_support^4
		min = 0
		max = GNG_legco_matsushita_seats
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_legco_faction_support^5
		min = 0
		max = GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_legco_faction_support^6
		min = 0
		max = GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_legco_faction_support^7
		min = 0
		max = GNG_legco_hitachi_seats
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_legco_faction_support
		index = i
		value = val

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { i < 8 } }
			round_variable = GNG_legco_faction_support^i
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Current_Ordinance_Votes_temp = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = GNG_legco_faction_support
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Current_Ordinance_Votes_temp = GNG_legco_faction_support^i }
	}
	set_variable = { GNG_Current_Ordinance_Votes = GNG_Current_Ordinance_Votes_temp }
}

GNG_check_legco_negative_seats = {
	## Makes sure there are no factions that has negative seats, monke code, but it works
	# - Scars
	set_temp_variable = { negative = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_yasuda_seats < 0 }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { negative = GNG_legco_yasuda_seats }
		set_variable = { GNG_legco_yasuda_seats = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_suzuki_seats < 0 }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { negative = GNG_legco_suzuki_seats }
		set_variable = { GNG_legco_suzuki_seats = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_seats < 0 }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { negative = GNG_legco_sony_seats }
		set_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_seats = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_seats < 0 }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { negative = GNG_legco_matsushita_seats }
		set_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_seats = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats < 0 }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { negative = GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats }
		set_variable = { GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats < 0 }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { negative = GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats }
		set_variable = { GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_hitachi_seats < 0 }
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { negative = GNG_legco_hitachi_seats }
		set_variable = { GNG_legco_hitachi_seats = 0 }
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = { negative = -1 }
	add_to_temp_array = { most_seats = GNG_legco_yasuda_seats }
	add_to_temp_array = { most_seats = GNG_legco_suzuki_seats }
	add_to_temp_array = { most_seats = GNG_legco_sony_seats }
	add_to_temp_array = { most_seats = GNG_legco_matsushita_seats }
	add_to_temp_array = { most_seats = GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats }
	add_to_temp_array = { most_seats = GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats }
	add_to_temp_array = { most_seats = GNG_legco_hitachi_seats }
	find_highest_in_array = {
		array = most_seats
		index = most
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = { most = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { most = 1 } }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_yasuda_seats = negative }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { most = 2 } }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_suzuki_seats = negative }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { most = 3 } }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_seats = negative }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { most = 4 } }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_seats = negative }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { most = 5 } }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats = negative }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { most = 6 } }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats = negative }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { most = 7 } }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_hitachi_seats = negative }
	}
}

GNG_legco_votes_initialize = {
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = GNG_legco_yasuda_temp_support
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = GNG_legco_suzuki_temp_support
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = GNG_legco_sony_temp_support
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = GNG_legco_matsushita_temp_support
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = GNG_legco_fujitsu_temp_support
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = GNG_legco_cheungkong_temp_support
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	clamp_temp_variable = {
		var = GNG_legco_hitachi_temp_support
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_yasuda_support = GNG_legco_yasuda_seats }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_yasuda_support = GNG_legco_yasuda_temp_support }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_suzuki_support = GNG_legco_suzuki_seats }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_suzuki_support = GNG_legco_suzuki_temp_support }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_sony_support = GNG_legco_sony_seats }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_sony_support = GNG_legco_sony_temp_support }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_matsushita_support = GNG_legco_matsushita_seats }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_matsushita_support = GNG_legco_matsushita_temp_support }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_fujitsu_support = GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_fujitsu_support = GNG_legco_fujitsu_temp_support }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_cheungkong_support = GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_cheungkong_support = GNG_legco_cheungkong_temp_support }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_hitachi_support = GNG_legco_hitachi_seats }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_hitachi_support = GNG_legco_hitachi_temp_support }
	round_temp_variable = GNG_yasuda_support
	round_temp_variable = GNG_suzuki_support
	round_temp_variable = GNG_sony_support
	round_temp_variable = GNG_matsushita_support
	round_temp_variable = GNG_fujitsu_support
	round_temp_variable = GNG_cheungkong_support
	round_temp_variable = GNG_hitachi_support

	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Current_Ordinance_Votes_temp = GNG_yasuda_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Current_Ordinance_Votes_temp = GNG_suzuki_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Current_Ordinance_Votes_temp = GNG_sony_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Current_Ordinance_Votes_temp = GNG_matsushita_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Current_Ordinance_Votes_temp = GNG_fujitsu_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Current_Ordinance_Votes_temp = GNG_cheungkong_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Current_Ordinance_Votes_temp = GNG_hitachi_support }

	set_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^1 = GNG_yasuda_support }
	set_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^2 = GNG_suzuki_support }
	set_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^3 = GNG_sony_support }
	set_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^4 = GNG_matsushita_support }
	set_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^5 = GNG_fujitsu_support }
	set_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^6 = GNG_cheungkong_support }
	set_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^7 = GNG_hitachi_support }
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GNG_hide_votes_ordinance }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_votes_initialize_percentages_tt
	}
	else = {
		clr_country_flag = GNG_hide_votes_ordinance
	}
	GNG_check_votes_legco = yes
}

GNG_legco_change_votes = {
	add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^GNG_legco_faction = GNG_temp_votes }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_votes_color = GNG_temp_votes }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_temp_votes < 0 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_votes = -1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_legco_remove_votes_tt
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_legco_add_votes_tt
	}
	GNG_check_votes_legco = yes
}

GNG_legco_change_votes_percentage = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_votes_percentage_modified = GNG_temp_votes_percentage }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction = 1 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_votes_percentage_modified = GNG_legco_yasuda_seats }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^GNG_legco_faction = GNG_temp_votes_percentage_modified }
		round_variable = GNG_legco_faction_support^GNG_legco_faction
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction = 2 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_votes_percentage_modified = GNG_legco_suzuki_seats }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^GNG_legco_faction = GNG_temp_votes_percentage_modified }
		round_variable = GNG_legco_faction_support^GNG_legco_faction
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction = 3 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_votes_percentage_modified = GNG_legco_sony_seats }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^GNG_legco_faction = GNG_temp_votes_percentage_modified }
		round_variable = GNG_legco_faction_support^GNG_legco_faction
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction = 4 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_votes_percentage_modified = GNG_legco_matsushita_seats }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^GNG_legco_faction = GNG_temp_votes_percentage_modified }
		round_variable = GNG_legco_faction_support^GNG_legco_faction
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction = 5 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_votes_percentage_modified = GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^GNG_legco_faction = GNG_temp_votes_percentage_modified }
		round_variable = GNG_legco_faction_support^GNG_legco_faction
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction = 6 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_votes_percentage_modified = GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^GNG_legco_faction = GNG_temp_votes_percentage_modified }
		round_variable = GNG_legco_faction_support^GNG_legco_faction
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction = 7 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_votes_percentage_modified = GNG_legco_hitachi_seats }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^GNG_legco_faction = GNG_temp_votes_percentage_modified }
		round_variable = GNG_legco_faction_support^GNG_legco_faction
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_temp_votes_percentage < 0 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_votes_percentage = -1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_legco_remove_votes_percentage_tt
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_legco_add_votes_percentage_tt
	}
	GNG_check_votes_legco = yes
}

legco_set_popularities = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { character = GNG_suzuki_teiichi }
					has_country_leader = { character = GNG_matsuzawa_takuji }
				}
			}
			set_popularities = {
				paternalism = var:GNG_legco_sony_seats
				paternalism_2 = var:GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats
				despotism = var:GNG_legco_yasuda_seats
				despotism_1 = var:GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats
				despotism_2 = var:GNG_legco_matsushita_seats
				fascism = var:GNG_legco_suzuki_seats
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_Ibuka_Fascism
			}
			set_popularities = {
				paternalism = var:GNG_legco_sony_seats
				paternalism_2 = var:GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats
				despotism = var:GNG_legco_matsushita_seats
				fascism = var:GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats
				fascism_3 = var:GNG_legco_hitachi_seats
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = GNG_morita_akio }
			}
			set_popularities = {
				paternalism = var:GNG_legco_sony_seats
				paternalism_2 = var:GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats
				despotism = var:GNG_legco_matsushita_seats
				despotism_1 = var:GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats
				fascism = var:GNG_legco_hitachi_seats
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = GNG_matsushita_masaharu }
			}
			set_popularities = {
				paternalism = var:GNG_legco_sony_seats
				paternalism_2 = var:GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats
				despotism = var:GNG_legco_matsushita_seats
				despotism_1 = var:GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats
				fascism = var:GNG_legco_hitachi_seats
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = GNG_ibuka_masaru }
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GNG_Ibuka_Fascism
				}
			}
			set_popularities = {
				paternalism = var:GNG_legco_sony_seats
				paternalism_2 = var:GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats
				despotism = var:GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats
				despotism_2 = var:GNG_legco_matsushita_seats
				fascism = var:GNG_legco_hitachi_seats
			}
		}
	}
}
legco_introduce_ordinance = {
	set_variable = { GNG_legco_current_ordinance_id = GNG_temp_legco_id }
	log = "Guangdong ID [?GNG_temp_legco_id] Bill Initialize"
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_legco_bill_introduce_tooltip
	GNG_legco_votes_initialize = yes
}

legco_ordinance_vote_start = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_legco_vote_days_special
			}
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_legco_vote_days = 30 }
	}
	clr_country_flag = GNG_legco_vote_days_special
	set_variable = { GNG_legco_current_voting = 1 }
	hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = GNG_legco.1
			days = 1
		}
		set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_GNG_LegCo_Bill }
		add_TNO_alert_unless_exists = yes
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_legco_bill_voting_tooltip
	log = "Guangdong ID [?GNG_temp_legco_id] Bill Vote Start"
}

legco_introduce_ordinance_start = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_legco_vote_days_special
			}
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_legco_vote_days = 30 }
	}
	clr_country_flag = GNG_legco_vote_days_special
	set_variable = { GNG_legco_current_voting = 1 }
	hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = GNG_legco.1
			days = 1
		}
		set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_GNG_LegCo_Bill }
		add_TNO_alert_unless_exists = yes
	}
	set_variable = { GNG_legco_current_ordinance_id = GNG_temp_legco_id }
	log = "Guangdong ID [?GNG_temp_legco_id] Bill Initialize"
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_legco_bill_introduce_start_tooltip
	GNG_legco_votes_initialize = yes
}

legco_bill_conclude = {
	clr_country_flag = GNG_show_effects_for_ordinance
	set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_GNG_LegCo_Bill }
	remove_TNO_alert = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_riots_negotiations_stall
		}
		clr_country_flag = GNG_riots_negotiations_stall
		country_event = { id = guangdong_RiotsNegotiations.9 days = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			GNG = {
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_Current_Ordinance_Votes > 49 }
			}
			log = "Guangdong ID [?GNG_legco_current_ordinance_id] Bill Passed"
			GNG_pass_ordinance = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_Current_Ordinance_Votes < 50 }
			}
			log = "Guangdong ID [?GNG_legco_current_ordinance_id] Bill Fails"
			GNG_fail_ordinance = yes
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_AI_Guarantee_Pass
			}
			clr_country_flag = GNG_AI_Guarantee_Pass
			GNG_pass_ordinance = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_AI_Guarantee_Fail
			}
			clr_country_flag = GNG_AI_Guarantee_Fail
			GNG_fail_ordinance = yes
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				75 = {
					GNG_pass_ordinance = yes
				}
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = GNG_AI_ORDINANCES
							option = GNG_AI_ORDINANCES_YES
						}
					}
					GNG_fail_ordinance = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

GNG_show_effects_for_ordinance = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_holding_value = GNG_legco_current_ordinance_id}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_legco_id = GNG_legco_holding_value }
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_show_effects_for_ordinance_tt
	effect_tooltip = {
		GNG_ordinances_effects = yes
	}
}

GNG_ordinances_effects = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_legco_id = GNG_legco_holding_value }
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { GNG_legco_current_ordinance_id > 0 }}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_legco_ordinance_effects_tt
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_temp_legco_id = 1 } #RLSO
		}
		TNO_worsen_max_workhours_policy_effectiveness_low = yes
		TNO_improve_minimum_wage_policy_effectiveness_low = yes
		every_owned_state = {
			set_temp_variable = { chi_app_temp = 1 }
			GNG_chinese_app_change = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = RLSO_replace_old_LSO_tt
		set_variable = { GNG_labor_standards_var = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_temp_legco_id = 10 } #Confidence Motion in CE Suzuki
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CE_suzuki_motion_effects
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_temp_legco_id = 11 } #Industrial Organization Ordinance
		}
		TNO_improve_industrial_expertise_low = yes
		TNO_improve_industrial_equipment_low = yes
		set_temp_variable = { econ_centralization_temp = 2 }
		econ_centralization_change = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_temp_legco_id = 12 } #Rural Development Ordinance
		}
		TNO_improve_agriculture_low = yes
		set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 0.3}
		econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { econ_centralization_temp = 2 }
		econ_centralization_change = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_temp_legco_id = 13 } #PWIO
		}
		set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 0.3}
		econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.40 }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		TNO_improve_admin_efficiency_med = yes
		set_temp_variable = { econ_centralization_temp = 2 }
		econ_centralization_change = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_temp_legco_id = 14 } #Industrial Development Ordinance
		}
		set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 0.3}
		econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_admin_costs_temp = 0.25 }
		GNG_admin_costs_change = yes
		TNO_improve_admin_efficiency_low = yes
		set_temp_variable = { econ_centralization_temp = 2 }
		econ_centralization_change = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_temp_legco_id = 15 } #Public Finance Ordinance
		}
		TNO_improve_income_taxation_policy_effectiveness_med = yes
		set_temp_variable = { money_reserves_temp = 0.35 }
		econ_money_reserves_change_raw_money = yes
		set_country_flag = GNG_public_finance_ordinance_passed
		set_temp_variable = { econ_centralization_temp = 3 }
		econ_centralization_change = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_temp_legco_id = 16 } #Financial Solvency and Liquidity Ordinance

	GNG_amendments_check = yes
}

	set_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_legco_id = GNG_legco_holding_value }
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_legco_ordinance_failed_tt
}

GNG_amendments_check = {
	#Checks the amendments and adds appropriate effects based on them
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_ordinance_id = GNG_legco_holding_value }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_amendment_id = GNG_legco_amendments_1^GNG_legco_ordinance_id }
	GNG_amendment_effects = yes
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_amendment_id = GNG_legco_amendments_2^GNG_legco_ordinance_id }
	GNG_amendment_effects = yes
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_amendment_id = GNG_legco_amendments_3^GNG_legco_ordinance_id }
	GNG_amendment_effects = yes
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_amendment_id = GNG_legco_amendments_4^GNG_legco_ordinance_id }
	GNG_amendment_effects = yes
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_amendment_id = GNG_legco_amendments_5^GNG_legco_ordinance_id }
	GNG_amendment_effects = yes
}

### THREE EVILS OF GUANGDONG ###
# Use temp vars and scripted effects to avoid tooltip spam!!!!

GNG_China_opinion_change = {
	add_to_variable = { GNG_China_Opinion = GNG_opinion_temp_var }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_opinion_temp_var < 0
			}
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_opinion_temp_var = -1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Chinese_opinion_change_decrease_tt
	}
	else = { custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Chinese_opinion_change_increase_tt }
	GNG_clamp_three_evils = yes
}

GNG_Japan_approval_change = {
	add_to_variable = { GNG_Japan_Approval = GNG_approval_temp_var }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_approval_temp_var < 0
			}
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_approval_temp_var = -1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Japanese_approval_change_decrease_tt
	}
	else = { custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Japanese_approval_change_increase_tt }
	GNG_clamp_three_evils = yes
}

GNG_Corruption_Change = {
	add_to_variable = { GNG_corruption_var = GNG_corruption_temp_var }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_corruption_temp_var < 0
			}
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_temp_var = -1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Three_Evils_change_decrease_tt
	}
	else = { custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Three_Evils_change_increase_tt }
	GNG_clamp_three_evils = yes
}

GNG_China_Opinion_Cap_Change = {
	add_to_variable = { GNG_China_Opinion_Cap_Base = GNG_China_cap_temp }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_China_cap_temp < 0 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_China_cap_temp = -1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Three_Evils_china_cap_decrease_tt
	}
	else = { custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Three_Evils_china_cap_increase_tt }
	GNG_clamp_three_evils = yes
}

GNG_Japan_Approval_Cap_Change = {
	add_to_variable = { GNG_Japan_Approval_Cap_Base = GNG_Japan_cap_temp }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_Japan_cap_temp < 0 }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_Japan_cap_temp = -1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Three_Evils_japan_cap_decrease_tt
	}
	else = { custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Three_Evils_japan_cap_increase_tt }
	GNG_clamp_three_evils = yes
}

GNG_clamp_three_evils = {
	add_to_variable = { GNG_3E_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	set_variable = { GNG_China_Opinion_Cap = GNG_China_Opinion_Cap_Base }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_China_Opinion_Cap = this.modifier@GNG_republic_of_china_opinion_cap } #Calculates the China Cap so that the cap doesnt go over 100 after applying modifiers
	set_variable = { GNG_Japan_Approval_Cap = GNG_Japan_Approval_Cap_Base }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_Japan_Approval_Cap = this.modifier@GNG_japanese_empire_opinion_cap } #Calculates the Japan Cap so that the cap doesnt go over 100 after applying modifiers

	clamp_variable = { var = GNG_Japan_Approval_Cap min = 0 max = 100 }
	clamp_variable = { var = GNG_China_Opinion_Cap min = 0 max = 100 }

	clamp_variable = { var = GNG_Japan_Approval min = 0 max = GNG_Japan_Approval_Cap }
	clamp_variable = { var = GNG_China_Opinion min = 0 max = GNG_China_Opinion_Cap }
	clamp_variable = { var = GNG_corruption_var min = 0 max = 100 }
	GNG_3E_calculate_effects = yes
	GNG_Three_Evils_calculate_arrows_y = yes
	GNG_corruption_calc = yes
}

GNG_Three_Evils_calculate_arrows_y = {
	#China cap
	set_variable = { GNG_Three_Evils_china_y = 2.7 }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_Three_Evils_china_y = GNG_China_Opinion_Cap }
	round_variable = GNG_Three_Evils_china_y
	multiply_variable = { GNG_Three_Evils_china_y = -1 }

	#Japan cap
	set_variable = { GNG_Three_Evils_japan_y = 2.7 }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_Three_Evils_japan_y = GNG_Japan_Approval_Cap }
	round_variable = GNG_Three_Evils_japan_y
	multiply_variable = { GNG_Three_Evils_japan_y = -1 }
}

	set_variable = { GNG_China_Opinion = 40 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Japan_Approval = 75 }
	set_country_flag = GNG_show_corruption_decisions
	set_variable = { GNG_3E_Corruption_button_frame = 2 }
	GNG_clamp_three_evils = yes
}

	clr_country_flag = GNG_show_china_opinion_decisions
	clr_country_flag = GNG_show_corruption_decisions
	clr_country_flag = GNG_show_japan_approval_decisions

	set_variable = { GNG_3E_China_button_frame = 1 }
	set_variable = { GNG_3E_Japan_button_frame = 1 }
}

### 3E Effects Script ###

GNG_3E_calculate_effects = {
	### Value startup
	## China
	set_variable = { GNG_3E_annual_GDP_growth = 0.1 }
	set_variable = { GNG_3E_chinese_govt_support = 0.2 }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_China_Opinion > 50 } }
		set_variable = { GNG_3E_police_growth = 1 }
		clear_variable =  GNG_3E_triads_growth
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { GNG_3E_triads_growth = 1 }
		clear_variable =  GNG_3E_police_growth
	}

	## Japan
	set_variable = { GNG_3E_GDP_growth = 1.5 }
	set_variable = { GNG_3E_japanese_govt_support = 0.2 }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Japan_Approval > 50 } }
		set_variable = { GNG_3E_Misc_costs = 1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_3E_Yakuza_growth = 1 }
		clear_variable = GNG_3E_Kenpeitai_growth
		clear_variable = GNG_3E_Misc_income
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { GNG_3E_Kenpeitai_growth = 1 }
		set_variable = { GNG_3E_Misc_income = 0.5 }
		clear_variable = GNG_3E_Misc_costs
		clear_variable = GNG_3E_Yakuza_growth
	}

	set_temp_variable = { China_opinion_temp = GNG_China_Opinion }
	set_temp_variable = { Japan_approval_temp = GNG_Japan_Approval }

	# Turn to percent /50 as well as 0-50 and 50-100, where 50 is 0, 0 is -100, 100 is 100
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { China_opinion_temp = 50 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { Japan_approval_temp = 50 }
	divide_temp_variable = { China_opinion_temp = 50 }
	divide_temp_variable = { Japan_approval_temp = 50 }

	### Start calculations
	## China
	multiply_variable = { GNG_3E_annual_GDP_growth = China_opinion_temp }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_3E_chinese_govt_support = China_opinion_temp }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_China_Opinion > 50 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_3E_police_growth = China_opinion_temp }
	}
	else = {
		multiply_temp_variable = { China_opinion_temp = -1 }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_3E_triads_growth = China_opinion_temp }
	}

	## Japan
	multiply_variable = { GNG_3E_GDP_growth = Japan_approval_temp }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_3E_japanese_govt_support = Japan_approval_temp }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Japan_Approval > 50 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_3E_Misc_costs = Japan_approval_temp }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_3E_Yakuza_growth = Japan_approval_temp }
	}
	else = {
		multiply_temp_variable = { Japan_approval_temp = -1 }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_3E_Kenpeitai_growth = Japan_approval_temp }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_3E_Misc_income = Japan_approval_temp }
	}

	GNG_calc_three_evils_modifier = yes
}

GNG_calc_three_evils_modifier = {
	set_variable = { kenpeitai_growth_quarterly_true = 1.25 }
	set_variable = { yakuza_growth_quarterly_true = 1.25 }
	set_variable = { triad_growth_quarterly_true = 1.25 }
	set_variable = { police_growth_quarterly_true = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = GNG_enable_harder_underworld }
		add_to_variable = { kenpeitai_growth_quarterly_true = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { yakuza_growth_quarterly_true = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { triad_growth_quarterly_true = 1 }
	}
	set_variable = { kenpeitai_growth_quarterly_var = modifier@GNG_kenpeitai_growth_modifier }
	set_variable = { yakuza_growth_quarterly_var = modifier@GNG_yakuza_growth_modifier }
	set_variable = { triad_growth_quarterly_var = modifier@GNG_triads_growth_modifier }
	set_variable = { police_growth_quarterly_var = modifier@GNG_police_growth_modifier }
	add_to_variable = { kenpeitai_growth_quarterly_var = kenpeitai_growth_quarterly_true }
	add_to_variable = { yakuza_growth_quarterly_var = yakuza_growth_quarterly_true }
	add_to_variable = { triad_growth_quarterly_var = triad_growth_quarterly_true }
	add_to_variable = { police_growth_quarterly_var = police_growth_quarterly_true }
}

GNG_CRR_Startup_Script = {
	set_country_flag = GNG_Yasuda_CRR_Active

	set_variable = { CRR_Morita_Akio_points_display = 1 }
	set_variable = { CRR_Matsushita_points_display = 1 }
	set_variable = { CRR_Ibuka_points_display = 1 }

	set_variable = { CRR_Morita_Akio_points = 0 }
	set_variable = { CRR_Matsushita_points = 0 }
	set_variable = { CRR_Ibuka_points = 0 }

	clear_array = Yasuda_CRR_Share
	add_to_array = { Yasuda_CRR_Share = 30 }
	add_to_array = { Yasuda_CRR_Share = 25 }
	add_to_array = { Yasuda_CRR_Share = 30 }
	add_to_array = { Yasuda_CRR_Share = 15 }
	set_variable = { CRR_Fujitsu_Frame = 45 }
	set_country_flag = CRR_Reserved_Exists

	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CRR_startup_tooltip
	add_to_variable = { GNG_CRR_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}

# Use these scripted effects to increase the points of a chief executive

#=== When Ibuka chooses the stupid option ; distributes 3% of the reserved share to Sony and Matsushita ===#
GNG_CRR_Fuck_Ibuka = {
	add_to_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share^0 = 3 }
	add_to_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share^1 = 3 }
	subtract_from_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share^3 = 6 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CRR_Fuck_Ibuka_tt
	set_variable = { CRR_Fujitsu_Frame = Yasuda_CRR_Share^2 }
	add_to_variable = { CRR_Fujitsu_Frame = Yasuda_CRR_Share^3 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_CRR_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}

GNG_CRR_Fuck_Morita = {

	add_to_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share^2 = 3 }
	subtract_from_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share^3 = 6 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CRR_Fuck_Morita_tt
	set_variable = { CRR_Fujitsu_Frame = Yasuda_CRR_Share^2 }
	add_to_variable = { CRR_Fujitsu_Frame = Yasuda_CRR_Share^3 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_CRR_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}

# This shall be triggered by the event prior to the plurality check
GNG_CRR_legco_plurality_check = {
	add_to_temp_array = { GNG_legco_plurality_check_array = GNG_legco_sony_seats }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_plurality_check_array^0 = GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats }
	add_to_temp_array = { GNG_legco_plurality_check_array = GNG_legco_matsushita_seats }
	add_to_temp_array = { GNG_legco_plurality_check_array = GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats }
	find_highest_in_array = {
		array = GNG_legco_plurality_check_array
		index = highestpluralityidx
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { highestpluralityidx = 0 } }
		hidden_effect = { GNG_CRR_add_morita_points = yes }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { highestpluralityidx = 1 } }
		hidden_effect = { GNG_CRR_add_matsushita_points = yes }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { highestpluralityidx = 2 } }
		hidden_effect = { GNG_CRR_add_ibuka_points = yes }
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CRR_legco_plurality_check_tt
	hidden_effect = { GNG_CRR_choose_victor = yes }
}

#=== FINAL POINTS COUNT ===#
###  R E T U R N   T O   M O N K E  ###

GNG_CRR_choose_victor = {
	add_to_temp_array = { GNG_CRR_final_victor = CRR_Morita_Akio_points }
	add_to_temp_array = { GNG_CRR_final_victor = CRR_Matsushita_points }
	add_to_temp_array = { GNG_CRR_final_victor = CRR_Ibuka_points }

	for_loop_effect = {
		end = 3

		find_highest_in_array = {
			array = GNG_CRR_final_victor
			index = finalvictoridx
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { GNG_CRR_final_victor_2 = finalvictoridx }
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_CRR_final_victor^finalvictoridx = -1 }
	}
	clear_temp_array = GNG_CRR_final_victor
	add_to_temp_array = { GNG_CRR_final_victor = CRR_Morita_Akio_points }
	add_to_temp_array = { GNG_CRR_final_victor = CRR_Matsushita_points }
	add_to_temp_array = { GNG_CRR_final_victor = CRR_Ibuka_points }

	add_to_temp_array = { GNG_legco_plurality_check_array = GNG_legco_sony_seats }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_plurality_check_array^0 = GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats }
	add_to_temp_array = { GNG_legco_plurality_check_array = GNG_legco_matsushita_seats }
	add_to_temp_array = { GNG_legco_plurality_check_array = GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats }

	set_temp_variable = { victor1idx = GNG_CRR_final_victor_2^0 }
	set_temp_variable = { victor2idx = GNG_CRR_final_victor_2^1 }
	set_temp_variable = { victor3idx = GNG_CRR_final_victor_2^2 }

	# TIEBREAKER #
	if = { # In the unlikely event of a 3 way tie
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_CRR_final_victor^victor1idx = GNG_CRR_final_victor^victor2idx }
			check_variable = { GNG_CRR_final_victor^victor1idx = GNG_CRR_final_victor^victor3idx }
			has_game_rule = { rule = GNG_PATH option = DEFAULT }
		}
		find_highest_in_array = {
			array = GNG_legco_plurality_check_array
			index = finaltiebreakidx
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { finaltiebreakidx = 0 } }
			GNG_CRR_add_morita_points = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { finaltiebreakidx = 1 } }
			GNG_CRR_add_matsushita_points = yes
		}
		else = {
			GNG_CRR_add_ibuka_points = yes
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_CRR_final_victor^victor1idx = GNG_CRR_final_victor^victor2idx }
			has_game_rule = { rule = GNG_PATH option = DEFAULT }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_plurality_check_array^victor3idx = -1 }
		find_highest_in_array = {
			array = GNG_legco_plurality_check_array
			index = finaltiebreakidx
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { finaltiebreakidx = 0 } }
			GNG_CRR_add_morita_points = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { finaltiebreakidx = 1 } }
			GNG_CRR_add_matsushita_points = yes
		}
		else = {
			GNG_CRR_add_ibuka_points = yes
		}
	}
	# TIEBREAKER END #

	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { CRR_Morita_Akio_points > CRR_Matsushita_points }
					check_variable = { CRR_Morita_Akio_points > CRR_Ibuka_points }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GNG_PATH option = DEFAULT }
				}
				has_game_rule = { rule = GNG_PATH option = GNG_PATH_THE_GADGETEER_OF_GUANGDONG }
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = guangdong.121
			days = 2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { CRR_Matsushita_points > CRR_Morita_Akio_points }
					check_variable = { CRR_Matsushita_points > CRR_Ibuka_points }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GNG_PATH option = DEFAULT }
				}
				has_game_rule = { rule = GNG_PATH option = GNG_PATH_THE_ASCENDANT_HEIR }
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = guangdong.122
			days = 2
		}
	}
	else = {
		country_event = {
			id = guangdong.123
			days = 2
		}
	}
}

### The way I coded this is that the variables have a roof of 100 even of its "true" value instead of the variables having no roof where the script caps the display to 100
### Everytime a variable is changed, the rest changes equally

## P.S.: CRR stands for CaRetakeR

# 0 is Cheung Kong/Sony
# 1 is Matsushita
# 2 is Fujitsu
# 3 is "Reserved"

# THIS SCRIPT MUSTN'T BE EXECUTED BY INDEPENDENTLY!
GNG_CRR_update = {
	divide_temp_variable = { CRR_temp = 2 }
	set_temp_variable = { CRR_Excess = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = Yasuda_CRR_Share
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { i = Yasuda_CRR_Share_i }
					check_variable = { i = 3 }
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share^i = CRR_temp }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share^i < 0 } }
			add_to_temp_variable = { CRR_Excess = Yasuda_CRR_Share^i }
			set_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share^i = 0 }
		}
	}
	add_to_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share^Yasuda_CRR_Share_i = CRR_Excess }
	set_variable = { CRR_Fujitsu_Frame = Yasuda_CRR_Share^2 }
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = CRR_Reserved_Exists }
		add_to_variable = { CRR_Fujitsu_Frame = Yasuda_CRR_Share^3 }
	}
	add_to_variable = { GNG_CRR_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}

GNG_CRR_Update_Sony = {
	set_temp_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share_i = 0 }

	if = {
		limit = {
			set_temp_variable = { CRR_future_value = Yasuda_CRR_Share^Yasuda_CRR_Share_i }
			add_to_temp_variable = { CRR_future_value = CRR_temp }
			check_variable = { var = CRR_future_value value = 0 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
		add_to_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share^0 = CRR_temp }

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { CRR_temp < 0 } }
			multiply_temp_variable = { CRR_temp = -1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CRR_CK_decrease
			multiply_temp_variable = { CRR_temp = -1 }
			else = { custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CRR_CK_increase }
		}
		GNG_CRR_update = yes
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CRR_CK_lowpoint_hit
	}
}

GNG_CRR_Update_Matsushita = {
	set_temp_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share_i = 1 }

	if = {
		limit = {
			set_temp_variable = { CRR_future_value = Yasuda_CRR_Share^Yasuda_CRR_Share_i }
			add_to_temp_variable = { CRR_future_value = CRR_temp }
			check_variable = { var = CRR_future_value value = 0 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
		add_to_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share^1 = CRR_temp }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { CRR_temp < 0 } }
			multiply_temp_variable = { CRR_temp = -1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CRR_MS_decrease
			multiply_temp_variable = { CRR_temp = -1 }
			else = { custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CRR_MS_increase }
		}
		GNG_CRR_update = yes
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CRR_MS_lowpoint_hit
	}
}

		}

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { CRR_temp < 0 } }
			multiply_temp_variable = { CRR_temp = -1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CRR_FJ_decrease
			multiply_temp_variable = { CRR_temp = -1 }
			else = { custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CRR_FJ_increase }
		}
		GNG_CRR_update = yes
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CRR_FJ_lowpoint_hit
	}
}

	add_to_variable = { GNG_CRR_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}

GNG_CRR_give_auction_to_fujitsu_scam = {
	set_temp_variable = { reserved_temp = Yasuda_CRR_Share^3 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { reserved_temp = 4 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CRR_give_auction_to_fujitsu_scam_tt
	add_to_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share^2 = reserved_temp }
	add_to_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share^0 = 2 }
	add_to_variable = { Yasuda_CRR_Share^1 = 2 }
	remove_from_array = { array = Yasuda_CRR_Share index = 3 }
	clr_country_flag = CRR_Reserved_Exists
	set_variable = { CRR_Fujitsu_Frame = Yasuda_CRR_Share^2 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_CRR_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
}

	set_country_flag = GNG_CRR_Cheung_Kong
	add_to_variable = { GNG_CRR_dirty_variable = 0.01 }

GNG_CRR_stage2_transfer_seats = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_CRR_transfer_seats_tt

	set_temp_variable = { Yasuda_seats = GNG_legco_yasuda_seats }
	set_temp_variable = { CK_Assets = Yasuda_CRR_Share^0 }
	set_temp_variable = { MS_Assets = Yasuda_CRR_Share^1 }

	divide_temp_variable = { CK_Assets = 100 }
	divide_temp_variable = { MS_Assets = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { CK_Assets = Yasuda_seats }
	multiply_temp_variable = { MS_Assets = Yasuda_seats }
	round_temp_variable = CK_Assets
	round_temp_variable = MS_Assets

	subtract_from_temp_variable = { Yasuda_seats = CK_Assets }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { Yasuda_seats = MS_Assets }
	set_temp_variable = { FJ_Assets = Yasuda_seats }

	set_variable = { GNG_legco_yasuda_seats = 0 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats = CK_Assets }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_seats = MS_Assets }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats = FJ_Assets }

	set_variable = { GNG_legco_hitachi_seats = GNG_legco_suzuki_seats }
	set_variable = { GNG_legco_suzuki_seats = 0 }

	set_country_flag = GNG_legco_stage_2

	GNG_rerender_legco = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_hail_hitachi_chosen
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_hail_hitachi_chosen_tt
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 7 }
		GNG_change_legco_seats = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_contact_cheung_kong_chosen
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_contact_cheung_kong_chosen_tt
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 6 }
		GNG_change_legco_seats = yes
	}
}

### Economy Shit

GNG_calculate_target_GDP = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Next_Year_Target_GDP_Var_tt = this.GDP }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Next_Year_Growth_Var_multiplier = GNG_Next_Year_Growth_Var_tt }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Next_Year_Growth_Var_multiplier = 1 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_Next_Year_Target_GDP_Var_tt = GNG_Next_Year_Growth_Var_multiplier }
	custom_effect_tooltip = guangdong_economic_targets_tooltip
	set_variable = { GNG_GDP_Goal = GNG_Next_Year_Target_GDP_Var_tt }
	set_variable = { GNG_Growth_Goal = GNG_Next_Year_Growth_Var_tt }
	GNG_update_graph_econ_goal = yes
}

GNG_target_gdp_check = {
	set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_GNG_Economy_Check_Soon }
	remove_TNO_alert = yes
	if = { #Effect for reaching GDP goal
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = this.GDP
				value = GNG_GDP_Goal
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 1 } #1963 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 2 } #1964 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 3 } #1965 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.5
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = GNG_Hitachi_Growth.1
					days = 15
				}
				country_event = {
					id = GNG_LegCo_Changes.1
					days = 30
				}
				country_event = {
					id = GNG_Underworld_Changes.1
					days = 45
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 4 } #1966 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 5 } #1967 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 6 } #1968 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 7 } #1969 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 8 } #1970 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 9 } #1971 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.7
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 10 } #1972 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.8
		}
	}
	else_if = { #Effect for missing GDP goal
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				this.GDP < GNG_GDP_Goal
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 1 } #1963 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 2 } #1964 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.4 #The event is hardcoded to be the same due to Yasuda Crisis
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 3 } #1965 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.6
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = GNG_Hitachi_Growth.1
					days = 15
				}
				country_event = {
					id = GNG_LegCo_Changes.1
					days = 30
				}
				country_event = {
					id = GNG_Underworld_Changes.1
					days = 45
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 4 } #1966 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 5 } #1967 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 6 } #1968 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 7 } #1969 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 8 } #1970 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 9 } #1971 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.7
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 10 } #1972 effect
			}
			country_event = GNG_Econ.8
		}
	}
	add_to_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 1 }
}

GNG_Underworld_Changes_Effect = {
	random_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { yak_spt_temp = 1.5 }
		GNG_yakuza_control_change = yes
	}
	random_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { yak_spt_temp = 1.5 }
		GNG_yakuza_control_change = yes
	}
	random_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { tri_spt_temp = 1.5 }
		GNG_triad_control_change = yes
	}
	random_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { tri_spt_temp = 1.5 }
		GNG_triad_control_change = yes
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_temp_Var = 2.5 }
	GNG_Corruption_Change = yes
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = GNG_enable_harder_underworld }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_because_expanded_underworld_tt
		random_owned_state = {
			set_temp_variable = { yak_spt_temp = 1.5 }
			GNG_yakuza_control_change = yes
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			set_temp_variable = { tri_spt_temp = 1.5 }
			GNG_triad_control_change = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_temp_Var = 1.5 }
		GNG_Corruption_Change = yes
	}
}

GNG_Full_LegCo_Changes_Effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 3 } #Morita
		}
		set_temp_variable = { state_seats = GNG_legco_sony_seats }
		add_to_temp_variable = { state_seats = GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_LegCo_changes_effect_sony_tt
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { state_seats < 30 } } #if under 30 seats, take away 1 easy seats.
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 4 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_target_temp = 3 }
			GNG_change_legco_seats_specific_1 = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_temp_var = 3 }
			GNG_Corruption_Change = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { state_seats < 35 } } #if 30-35 seats, take away 2 easy seats.
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 4 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_target_temp = 3 }
			GNG_change_legco_seats_specific_1 = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_target_temp = 3 }
			GNG_change_legco_seats_specific_1 = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_temp_var = 3 }
			GNG_Corruption_Change = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { state_seats < 40 } } #if 35-40 seats, take away 2 hard seats.
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 7 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_target_temp = 3 }
			GNG_change_legco_seats_specific_1 = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_target_temp = 3 }
			GNG_change_legco_seats_specific_1 = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_temp_var = 3 }
			GNG_Corruption_Change = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { state_seats < 45 } } #if 40-45 seats, take away 3 seats.
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 7 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_target_temp = 3 }
			GNG_change_legco_seats_specific_1 = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_target_temp = 3 }
			GNG_change_legco_seats_specific_1 = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 4 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_target_temp = 6 }
			GNG_change_legco_seats_specific_1 = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_corruption_temp_var = 3 }
			GNG_Corruption_Change = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { state_seats < 50 } } #if 45-50 seats, take away 4 seats.
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 7 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_target_temp = 3 }
			GNG_change_legco_seats_specific_1 = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_target_temp = 3 }
			GNG_change_legco_seats_specific_1 = yes

			GNG_change_legco_seats = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = GNG_panic_legco_hitachi }
				check_variable = { GNG_legco_hitachi_seats > 50 }
			}
			set_country_flag = GNG_panic_legco_hitachi
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = GNG_LegCo_Changes.103
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
	}
}


GNG_hit_GDP_target_effect = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_seat_temp = 3 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_temp = GNG_legco_faction_in_power }
	GNG_change_legco_seats = yes
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Next_Year_Growth_Var_tt = GNG_Base_Expected_Growth }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_enabled_higher_growth_expectations
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Next_Year_Growth_Var_tt = 0.015 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Base_Expected_Growth = 0.015 }
	}
	else = {
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Next_Year_Growth_Var_tt = 0.01 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Base_Expected_Growth = 0.01 }
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { jap_app_temp = 2 }
		GNG_japanese_app_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { zhu_app_temp = 1.5 }
		GNG_zhujin_app_change = yes
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_approval_temp_var = 5 }
	GNG_Japan_approval_change = yes
	GNG_calculate_target_GDP = yes
	add_to_variable = { GNG_GDP_target_met_tracker = 1 }
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 4 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_GDP_matsushita_target_met_tracker = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { GNG_tokyo_meetings_counter = 6 } }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { GNG_GDP_matsushita_target_met_tracker > 1 } }
					country_event = {
						id = guangdong_matsushitaflavor.58
						days = 15
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { GNG_GDP_matsushita_target_met_tracker < 2 } }
					country_event = {
						id = guangdong_matsushitaflavor.59
						days = 15
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	GNG_calculate_target_GDP = yes

						days = 15
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { GNG_GDP_matsushita_target_met_tracker < 2 } }
					country_event = {
						id = guangdong_matsushitaflavor.59
						days = 15
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

GNG_calculate_rGDP = {
	set_variable = { GNG_rGDP_debuff = this.modifier@GNG_rGDP_modifier }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_rGDP_debuff
		max = 0
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = TNO_has_started_up }
		update_economy_tab = yes
	}
}

GNG_calculate_fiscal_health = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				debt_to_GDP_ratio < 0.251
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_fiscal_status_var_temp = 0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				debt_to_GDP_ratio < 0.501
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_fiscal_status_var_temp = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				debt_to_GDP_ratio < 0.31
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_fiscal_status_var_temp = 2 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				debt_to_GDP_ratio < 1.001
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_fiscal_status_var_temp = 3 }
	}
	else = {
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_fiscal_status_var_temp = 4 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_disable_all_mechanics_IJA
			}
		}
		GNG_update_fiscal = yes
	}
}

GNG_yasuda_crisis_effects = {
	add_to_variable = { national_debt = 3.85 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_enabled_higher_debt
		}
		add_to_variable = { national_debt = 2.5 }
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_state = {
			multiply_variable = {
				state_value = 0.88
			}
		}
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_yasuda_crisis_economic_crisis
	subtract_from_variable = { gdp_growth = 2.5 }
	add_to_variable = { base_inflation_rate = 2.25 }
	calculate_debt_to_GDP_ratio = yes
	every_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { jap_app_temp = -3 }
		GNG_japanese_app_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { zhu_app_temp = -2 }
		GNG_zhujin_app_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { chi_app_temp = -1 }
		GNG_chinese_app_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { sar_spt_temp = -2.5 }
		GNG_police_control_change = yes
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_general_status_var_temp = 1 }
	GNG_update_status = yes
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_security_status_var_temp = 5 }
	GNG_update_security = yes
	set_variable = { GNG_Base_Expected_Growth = 0.06 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_enabled_higher_growth_expectations
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Base_Expected_Growth = 0.015 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_enabled_lower_growth_expectations
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Base_Expected_Growth = -0.01 }
	}
	set_country_flag = yasuda_crisis
	mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	recalculate_GDP_and_PUs_on_demand = yes
	calculate_debt_to_GDP_ratio = yes
	GNG_calculate_rGDP = yes
	update_economy_tab = yes
}

GNG_oil_crisis_effects = {
	add_to_variable = { national_debt = 1.75 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_enabled_higher_debt
		}
		add_to_variable = { national_debt = 2.5 }
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_oil_crisis_economic_crisis
	clr_country_flag = GNG_desparate_economic_decisions_unlocked
	clr_country_flag = GNG_silicon_years_active
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_outraced_manchukuo
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_race_with_manchukuo_on_hold_OC_tt
	}
	subtract_from_variable = { gdp_growth = 5.5 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 7 } #Hitachi
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { gdp_growth = 1 }
	}
	add_to_variable = { base_inflation_rate = 3 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Base_Expected_Growth = 0.05 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 3 } #Sony
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_commonOC.2
				days = 7
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_temp_variable = { jap_app_temp = -3 }
				GNG_japanese_app_change = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_approval_temp_var = -7.5 }
			GNG_Japan_approval_change = yes
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_japanese_empire_cap = -10 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_OC_sony_debuff
		load_focus_tree = GNG_morita_oil_crisis_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 4 } #Matsushita
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_commonOC.3
				days = 7
			}
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_approval_temp_var = -7.5 }
			GNG_Japan_approval_change = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_opinion_temp_var = -7.5 }
			GNG_China_opinion_change = yes
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_republic_of_china_cap = -5 }
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_japanese_empire_cap = -5 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_OC_matsushita_debuff
		load_focus_tree = GNG_matsushita_oil_crisis_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 5 } #Fujitsu
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_commonOC.4
				days = 7
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_temp_variable = { chi_app_temp = -3 }
				GNG_chinese_app_change = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_opinion_temp_var = -7.5 }
			GNG_China_opinion_change = yes
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_republic_of_china_cap = -10 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_OC_fujitsu_debuff
		load_focus_tree = GNG_ibuka_oil_crisis_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 7 } #Hitachi
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_hitachiOC.4
				days = 4
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_temp_variable = { chi_app_temp = -3 }
				GNG_chinese_app_change = yes
				set_temp_variable = { zhu_app_temp = -3 }
				GNG_zhujin_app_change = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_opinion_temp_var = -7.5 }
			GNG_China_opinion_change = yes
			set_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_republic_of_china_cap = -10 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_OC_hitachi_debuff
		load_focus_tree = GNG_komai_oil_crisis_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_general_status_var_temp = 3 }
	GNG_update_status = yes
	set_country_flag = GNG_oil_crisis
	hidden_effect = {
		recalculate_GDP_and_PUs_on_demand = yes
		calculate_debt_to_GDP_ratio = yes
		GNG_calculate_rGDP = yes
		update_economy_tab = yes
		GNG_stall_ordinance = yes
	}
	GNG_product_cycle_var_calc = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_political_power > 500
		}
		set_political_power = 500
	}
}

### RIOTS ###

GNG_initialize_riots = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_riots_begin_tt
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_general_status_var_temp = 4 }
	GNG_update_status = yes
	set_variable = { GNG_Base_Expected_Growth = 0.05 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 3 #Sony
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = 45 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 45 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism = 25 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism = 35 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair = 15 }
		set_country_flag = { flag = GNG_riots_60_day_limiter value = 1 days = 60 }
		set_country_flag = { flag = GNG_riots_240_day_limiter value = 1 days = 240 }

		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick_base = 3 }
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick_base = 2.5 }
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick_base = 3.5 }
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick_base = 3.5 }
		randomize_variable = {
			var = riot_growth_next
			distribution = uniform
			min = 1
			max = 4.49 #Oddly specific value is to make sure that 3.5 and 4 are more normal values
		}
		round_variable = riot_growth_next
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { riot_growth_next > 1 } } #This is to generate x.5 or x.0 values
			random_list = {
				1 = {

				}
				1 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { riot_growth_next = 0.5 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_Map_Changes_Triad_Ally_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_China_Opinion < 50 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = 5 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 5 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism = 7.5 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism = 7.5 }
			set_country_flag = GNG_Chinese_intervention
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Chinese_intervention_active
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_zhu_app < 50 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = 10 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism = 7.5 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Zhujin_anger_GFT_strength_radicalism
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_chi_app < 50 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 10 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism = 7.5 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Chinese_anger_CCL_strength_radicalism
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { total_national_zhu_pop_percent < 0.2 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 10 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_low_zhujin_pop_CCL_strength
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = 100 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = GNG_Japan_Approval }
		divide_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = 2 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Japanese_Frustration_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_jap_app < 65 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots = 10 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_japan_anger_frustration_increase
		}
		load_focus_tree = GNG_morita_riots
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 4 #Matsushita
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = 50 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 50 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism = 35 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism = 45 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair = 15 }

		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick_base = 3.5 }
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick_base = 2.5 }
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick_base = 3.5 }
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick_base = 3 }
		randomize_variable = {
			var = riot_growth_next
			distribution = uniform
			min = 1
			max = 4.49 #Oddly specific value is to make sure that 3.5 and 4 are more normal values
		}
		round_variable = riot_growth_next
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { riot_growth_next > 1 } } #This is to generate x.5 or x.0 values
			random_list = {
				1 = {

				}
				1 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { riot_growth_next = 0.5 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GNG = {
					has_country_flag = GNG_matsushita_yakuza_ally
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_Map_Changes_Yakuza_Ally_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				GNG = {
					has_country_flag = GNG_matsushita_triad_ally
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_Map_Changes_Triad_Ally_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_Map_Changes_No_Ally_tt
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_China_Opinion < 50 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = 5 }
			add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = 5 }

GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Change = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_GFT_OVER
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { amount = GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp < 0 } }
			multiply_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_decrease_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_increase_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp }
		GNG_Riots_var_calc = yes
	}
}
GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Change = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_GFT_OVER
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { amount = GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Temp }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Temp < 0 } }
			multiply_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_decrease_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_increase_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism = GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Temp }
		GNG_Riots_var_calc = yes
	}
}

			check_variable = { GNG_Proposal_Value = 60 }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = guangdong_RiotsNegotiations.13
			days = 3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_Proposal_Value = 70 }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = guangdong_RiotsNegotiations.14
			days = 3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_Proposal_Value = 80 }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = guangdong_RiotsNegotiations.15
			days = 3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_Proposal_Value = 90 }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = guangdong_RiotsNegotiations.16
			days = 3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_Proposal_Value = 100 }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = guangdong_RiotsNegotiations.17
			days = 3
		}
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_GFT_negotiated_tt
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_CCL_OVER
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_selected_riot_group = 0 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { GNG_selected_riot_group = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick_Temp = -1 }
		GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick_Change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick_Temp = -1 }
		GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick_Change = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_tick_dealt_with_CCL_increase_tt
	}
	set_country_flag = GFT_Dismantled_Negotiation
	set_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_GFT_OVER
	set_variable = { GNG_riot_group_negotiating = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism = 0 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength = 0 }
	every_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { govt_spt_temp = 5 }
		GNG_government_control_change = yes
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Temp = -60 }
	GNG_Despair_Change = yes
	add_political_power = 75
	set_variable = { GNG_Proposal_Value = 0 }
}

GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Change = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_CCL_OVER
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { amount = GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Temp }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Temp < 0 } }
			multiply_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_decrease_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_increase_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength = GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Temp }
		GNG_Riots_var_calc = yes
	}
}

GNG_Riots_var_calc = {
	GNG_Riots_Strength_Total_Calc = yes
	GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total_Calc = yes
	GNG_Riots_GFT_AVG_Calc = yes
	GNG_Riots_CCL_AVG_Calc = yes
	GNG_Riots_Despair_Calc = yes
	GNG_Japan_Riots_Calc = yes
	GNG_Calc_Ticks = yes
}

GNG_Calc_Ticks = {
	GNG_update_underworld_display = yes
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick = GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick_base }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick = GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick_base }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick = GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick_base }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick = GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick_base }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick = modifier@GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick_modifier }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick = modifier@GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick_modifier }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick = modifier@GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick_modifier }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick = modifier@GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick_modifier }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick
		min = 0
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick
		min = 0
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick
		min = 0
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick
		min = 0
	}
}

GNG_Riots_Strength_Total_Calc = {
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Total_Temp = GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Total_Temp = GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength }
	divide_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Total_Temp = 2 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Strength_Total = GNG_Riots_Strength_Total_Temp }
}

GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total_Calc = {
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total_Temp = GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total_Temp = GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism }
	divide_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total_Temp = 2 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total = GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total_Temp }
}

GNG_Riots_GFT_AVG_Calc = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_AVG_Calc_Temp = GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_AVG_Calc_Temp = GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_AVG = GNG_Riots_GFT_AVG_Calc_Temp }
}

GNG_Riots_CCL_AVG_Calc = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_AVG_Calc_Temp = GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength }
	add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_AVG_Calc_Temp = GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism }
	set_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_AVG = GNG_Riots_CCL_AVG_Calc_Temp }
}

GNG_Riots_Despair_Calc = {
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Riots_Despair
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair > 66 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair > 33 }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick = 0.5 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick = 0 }
	}
}

GNG_Japan_Riots_Calc = {
	clamp_variable = {
		var = GNG_Japan_Riots
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
}

GNG_fire_riots_event = {
	random_list = { # should a protestor or police event fire
		var:GNG_riot_event_chance = { # set in guangdong_commonRiots.1001
			GNG_riots_fire_terror_event = yes
		}
		1 = {
			GNG_riots_fire_police_event = yes
		}
	}
	random_list = { # sets the target group for the upcoming event. Would use random lists in the events but the tooltip doesn't look nice
		1 = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_GFT_OVER
			}
			set_variable = { GNG_riot_event_target = 0 }
		}
		1 = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_CCL_OVER
			}
			set_variable = { GNG_riot_event_target = 1 }
		}
	}
}

GNG_riots_fire_terror_event = {
	if = { # has terror flag
		limit = { has_country_flag = GNG_riots_terror_active }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.128 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.129 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.130 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.131 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.132 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = { # low radicalism
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total < 33 } }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.100 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.101 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.102 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.103 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.104 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.105 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.106 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = { # high radicalism
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Total > 66 } }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.118 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.119 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.120 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.121 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.122 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.123 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.124 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
	}
	else = { # med radicalism
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.109 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.110 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.111 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.112 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.113 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.114 hours = 6 }
			}
			1 = {
				country_event = { id = guangdong_commonRiots.115 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
	}
}

GNG_riots_police_event_effects = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Temp = -3 }
	GNG_Despair_Change = yes
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_riot_event_target = 0 } }
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp = -3 }
		GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Temp = -1.5 }
		GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Change = yes
	}
	else = {
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Temp = -3 }
		GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism_Temp = -1.5 }
		GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism_Change = yes
	}
	random_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { govt_spt_temp = 2 }
		GNG_government_control_change = yes
	}
	random_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { govt_spt_temp = 2 }
		GNG_government_control_change = yes
	}
	clear_variable = GNG_riot_event_target
}

	GNG_Japanese_Intervention_Change = yes

GNG_riots_event_effects_terror = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Temp = 5 }
	GNG_Despair_Change = yes
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_riot_event_target = 0 } }
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Temp = 3 }
		GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp = 4.5 }
		GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Change = yes
	}
	else = {
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism_Temp = 3 }
		GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism_Change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Temp = 4.5 }
		GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Change = yes
	}
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots_Temp = 2 }
	GNG_Japanese_Intervention_Change = yes
	random_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { riot_spt_temp = 4 }
		GNG_rioters_control_change = yes
	}
	random_owned_state = {
		set_temp_variable = { riot_spt_temp = 4 }
		GNG_rioters_control_change = yes
	}
	clear_variable = GNG_riot_event_target
}

								hog_the_dispersing_clouds
							}
							ledger = civilian
							cost = -1
						}
					}
				}
				GNG_komai_kenichiro = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { small = "GFX_idea_GNG_minister_Komai_Kenichiro_70s" }
					}
					remove_advisor_role = { slot = foreign_minister }
					add_advisor_role = {
						advisor = {
							slot = foreign_minister
							idea_token = GNG_Komai_Kenichiro_70s_2_for
							traits = {
								foreign_minister
								for_here_to_stay
							}
							ledger = civilian
							cost = -1
						}
					}
				}
				add_ideas = {
					GNG_Matsushita_Masaharu_Ibuka_70s_2_hog
					GNG_Komai_Kenichiro_70s_2_for
				}
				set_country_flag = GNG_ibuka_reconciliation_achievement
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 7 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_hitachi_manchukuoending
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				GNG_komai_kenichiro = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/GNG/GNG_Komai_Kenichiro_70s_Manchurian.dds" }
					}
				}
				set_country_leader_description = {
					desc = "POLITICS_KOMAI_KENICHIRO_70S_MANCHURIAN_DESC"
				}
				remove_advisor_role = { slot = foreign_minister }
				add_advisor_role = {
					advisor = {
						slot = foreign_minister
						idea_token = GNG_Matsushita_Masaharu_Komai_70s_1_for
						traits = {
							foreign_minister
							for_a_string_of_strings
						}
						ledger = civilian
						cost = -1
					}
				}
				add_ideas = {
					GNG_Matsushita_Masaharu_Komai_70s_1_for
				}
				set_country_flag = GNG_komai_manchurian_achievement
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_hitachi_manchukuo_ending_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_hitachi_komaiending
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				GNG_komai_kenichiro = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/GNG/GNG_Komai_Kenichiro_70s_Personalist.dds" }
					}
				}
				set_country_leader_description = {
					desc = "POLITICS_KOMAI_KENICHIRO_70S_PERSONALIST_DESC"
				}
				GNG_matsushita_masaharu = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { small = "GFX_idea_GNG_minister_Matsushita_Masaharu_70s" }
					}
					remove_advisor_role = { slot = foreign_minister }
					add_advisor_role = {
						advisor = {
							slot = foreign_minister
							idea_token = GNG_Matsushita_Masaharu_Komai_70s_2_for
							traits = {

							cost = -1

					}

					GNG_Matsushita_Masaharu_Komai_70s_2_for
				}
				set_country_flag = GNG_komai_independent_achievement
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_hitachi_komai_ending_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_trait = {
					character = GNG_komai_kenichiro
					trait = the_manchurian_executive
					ideology = fascism_reform_bureaucracy_subtype
				}
				add_trait = {
					character = GNG_komai_kenichiro
					trait = guangdongs_caesar
					ideology = fascism_reform_bureaucracy_subtype
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = GNG_do_as_i_say
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = GNG_the_house_always_wins }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_hitachiRiots.19
				days = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = GNG_not_as_i_do
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = GNG_i_play_this_game_best }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_hitachiRiots.22
				days = 1
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = guangdong_hitachiRiots.62
			days = 5
		}
	}
	clr_country_flag = GNG_Riots_Active
	clr_country_flag = GNG_Riots_Show_GUI
	clr_country_flag = GNG_riots_terror_active
	clr_country_flag = GNG_IJA_InterventionPossible
	add_to_variable = { GNG_map_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_product_decisions_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_3E_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_economy_dirty_variable = 0.01 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 3 #Sony
			}
		}
		load_focus_tree = GNG_morita_ending_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}

	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 4 #Matsushita
			}
		}
		load_focus_tree = GNG_matsushita_epilogue_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}


	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 5 #Fujitsu
			}
		}
		load_focus_tree = GNG_ibuka_ending_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}

	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 7 #Hitachi
			}
		}
		load_focus_tree = GNG_komai_ending_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_general_status_var_temp = 2 }
		GNG_update_status = yes
		remove_mission = GNG_the_situation_updates
		set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 3.5 }
		econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
	}
	GNG_unload_underworld_stats = yes
}
