GNG_Arms_Market_Product_Select = {
	set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_arms_market_price_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_country_selected = 0 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_Arms_Market_Japan_Sales_Multiplier^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_country_selected = 1 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_Arms_Market_China_Sales_Multiplier^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_country_selected = 2 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_Arms_Market_Indonesia_Sales_Multiplier^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_country_selected = 3 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_Arms_Market_Free_Indonesia_Sales_Multiplier^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_country_selected = 4 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_Arms_Market_Thailand_Sales_Multiplier^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_country_selected = 5 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_Arms_Market_Azad_Hind_Sales_Multiplier^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_country_selected = 6 } }
		multiply_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price = GNG_Arms_Market_Shonan_Sales_Multiplier^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	}
	set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_active_price_mil = GNG_arms_market_active_price }
	multiply_variable = {GNG_arms_market_active_price_mil = 1000 }

	set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_product_quantity = GNG_arms_market_quantity_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }

	set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_product_activity = GNG_arms_market_activity_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }

	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_arms_market_activity_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected > GNG_arms_market_total_activity } }
		set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_option_button = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_arms_market_id_temp = GNG_arms_market_product_tech_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
			check_variable = { num_equipment@var:GNG_arms_market_id_temp < GNG_arms_market_quantity_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
		}
		set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_option_button = 2 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^GNG_arms_market_country_selected < GNG_arms_market_price_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected } }
		set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_option_button = 3 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_option_button = 4 }
	}
}

GNG_Arms_Market_Sell_Product = {
	set_temp_variable = { money_reserves_temp = GNG_arms_market_active_price }
	econ_money_reserves_change_raw_money = yes
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Sales_Temp = GNG_arms_market_product_tech_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_arms_Market_eq_loss_temp = GNG_arms_market_quantity_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_arms_Market_eq_loss_temp = -1 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_arms_Market_eq_gain_temp = GNG_arms_market_quantity_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }

	GNG = {
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = var:GNG_Arms_Market_Sales_Temp
			amount = GNG_arms_Market_eq_loss_temp
			producer = GNG
		}
	}

	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Target_Var = GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Scope_List^GNG_arms_market_country_selected }


	var:GNG_Arms_Market_Target_Var = {
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = var:GNG.GNG_Arms_Market_Sales_Temp
			amount = GNG.GNG_arms_Market_eq_gain_temp
			producer = GNG
		}
	}

	subtract_from_variable = { GNG_arms_market_total_activity = GNG_arms_market_activity_list^GNG_arms_market_product_selected }
	subtract_from_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^GNG_arms_market_country_selected = GNG_arms_market_active_price }

	GNG_Arms_Market_Product_Select = yes
}

GNG_Arms_Market_Yearly_Refresh = {
	set_variable = { GNG_arms_market_total_activity = 100 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^0 = 1 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^1 = 0.6 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^2 = 0.4 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^3 = 0.4 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^4 = 0.3 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^5 = 0.3 }
	set_variable = { GNG_Arms_Market_Country_Money_List^6 = 0.15 }
}

GNG_ibuka_trademark_passed_support = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_the_guangdong_trademark_ordinance_passed
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_temp_support = -0.2 } #1 = 100%
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_cheungkong_temp_support = -0.2 } #1 = 100%
	}
}

GNG_ibuka_anti_corruption_passed_support = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_ibuka_anti_corruption_passed
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GNG_ibuka_anti_corruption_2_passed
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_temp_support = 0.05 } #1 = 100%
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_temp_support = 0.1 } #1 = 100%
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_cheungkong_temp_support = 0.05 } #1 = 100%
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_temp_votes_percentage = 0.1 } #1 = 100%
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_ibuka_anti_corruption_2_passed
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_temp_support = -0.1 } #1 = 100%
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_temp_support = 0.1 } #1 = 100%
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_cheungkong_temp_support = -0.1 } #1 = 100%
		add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_hitachi_temp_support = 0.1 } #1 = 100%
	}
}

GNG_ibuka_modern_police_passed_support = {

GNG_test = {
	randomize_variable = {
		var = riot_growth_next
		distribution = uniform
		min = 1
		max = 4.49
	}
	round_variable = riot_growth_next
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { riot_growth_next > 1 }
			} #This is to generate x.5 or x.0 values
			random_list = {
				1 = {

				}
				1 = {
					subtract_from_variable = { riot_growth_next = 0.5 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		start = 1
		end = 11
		value = v

	}
	set_variable = { GNG_Proposals_Current_Selected_Proposal = 0 }
	set_country_flag = GNG_Negotiations_Proposals_Visible
}

GNG_negotiations_add_seats = {
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_fujitsu_check = GNG_legco_fujitsu_seats }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_fujitsu_check = GNG_legco_faction_support^5 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_check = GNG_legco_matsushita_seats }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_check = GNG_legco_faction_support^4 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_check = GNG_legco_sony_seats }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_check = GNG_legco_faction_support^3 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check = GNG_legco_cheungkong_seats }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check = GNG_legco_faction_support^6 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_hitachi_check = GNG_legco_hitachi_seats }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { GNG_legco_hitachi_check = GNG_legco_faction_support^7 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 3 } #Sony
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_check < GNG_votes_needed }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^3 = GNG_legco_sony_check }
			subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_sony_check }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check < GNG_votes_needed }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^6 = GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check }
				subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_check < GNG_votes_needed }
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^4 = GNG_legco_matsushita_check }
					subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_matsushita_check }
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { GNG_legco_fujitsu_check < GNG_votes_needed }
						}
						add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^5 = GNG_legco_fujitsu_check }
						subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_fujitsu_check }
						add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^7 = GNG_votes_needed }
					}
					else = {
						add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^5 = GNG_votes_needed }
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^4 = GNG_votes_needed }
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^6 = GNG_votes_needed }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^3 = GNG_votes_needed }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_in_power = 4 } #Matsushita
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GNG_legco_matsushita_check < GNG_votes_needed }
			}
			add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^4 = GNG_legco_matsushita_check }
			subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_matsushita_check }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check < GNG_votes_needed }
				}
				add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^6 = GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check }
				subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_cheung_kong_check }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GNG_legco_sony_check < GNG_votes_needed }
					}
					add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^3 = GNG_legco_sony_check }
					subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_sony_check }
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { GNG_legco_fujitsu_check < GNG_votes_needed }
						}
						add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^5 = GNG_legco_fujitsu_check }
						subtract_from_variable = { GNG_votes_needed = GNG_legco_fujitsu_check }
						add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^7 = GNG_votes_needed }
					}
					else = {

					}
				}
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^3 = GNG_votes_needed }
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^6 = GNG_votes_needed }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { GNG_legco_faction_support^4 = GNG_votes_needed }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {

		}

GNG_IJA_piechart_manipulation = {
	set_temp_variable = { party_pop_multiplier = 1 }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_takeover_party_pop_calc = GNG_IJA_takeover_party_pop }
	divide_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_takeover_party_pop_calc = 100 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { party_pop_multiplier = GNG_IJA_takeover_party_pop_calc }

	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_paternalism_holding_calc = GNG_IJA_paternalism_holding }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_paternalism_2_holding_calc = GNG_IJA_paternalism_2_holding }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_holding_calc = GNG_IJA_despotism_holding }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_1_holding_calc = GNG_IJA_despotism_1_holding }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_2_holding_calc = GNG_IJA_despotism_2_holding }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_fascism_holding_calc = GNG_IJA_fascism_holding }
	set_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_fascism_3_holding_calc = GNG_IJA_fascism_3_holding }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_paternalism_holding_calc = party_pop_multiplier }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_paternalism_2_holding_calc = party_pop_multiplier }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_holding_calc = party_pop_multiplier }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_1_holding_calc = party_pop_multiplier }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_2_holding_calc = party_pop_multiplier }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_fascism_holding_calc = party_pop_multiplier }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_fascism_3_holding_calc = party_pop_multiplier }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_paternalism_holding_calc = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_paternalism_2_holding_calc = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_holding_calc = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_1_holding_calc = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_despotism_2_holding_calc = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_fascism_holding_calc = 100 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { GNG_IJA_fascism_3_holding_calc = 100 }

	set_popularities = {
		paternalism = var:GNG_IJA_paternalism_holding_calc
		paternalism_2 = var:GNG_IJA_paternalism_2_holding_calc
		despotism = var:GNG_IJA_despotism_holding_calc
		despotism_1 = var:GNG_IJA_despotism_1_holding_calc
		despotism_2 = var:GNG_IJA_despotism_2_holding_calc
		fascism = var:GNG_IJA_fascism_holding_calc
		fascism_3 = var:GNG_IJA_fascism_3_holding_calc
		ultranationalism = var:GNG_IJA_takeover_party_pop
	}
}

GNG_IJA_add_takeover_progress = {
	add_to_variable = { GNG_IJA_takeover_progress = v }
	clamp_variable = { var = GNG_IJA_takeover_progress min = 0 max = 100 }

	set_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = GNG_IJA_takeover_progress }
	divide_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = 491 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = -8 }
	clamp_variable = { var = GNG_IJA_bar_x min = 8 max = 464 }

}

GNG_IJA_remove_takeover_progress = {
	add_to_variable = { GNG_IJA_takeover_progress = v }
	clamp_variable = { var = GNG_IJA_takeover_progress min = 0 max = 100 }

	set_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = GNG_IJA_takeover_progress }
	divide_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = 100 }
	multiply_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = 491 }
	add_to_variable = { GNG_IJA_bar_x = -8 }
	clamp_variable = { var = GNG_IJA_bar_x min = 8 max = 464 }
}
